<pics>None< /pics><resp>None<//resp><GmapID>0x808586d4a5f2b22b:0xa4b7db1e11009f09<//GmapID></record></dataset><record>
< Text>
Perfect location if you're touring around the Embarcadero in San Francisco. It's right before Crissy Field, the restored wetlands that leads up to Ft. Point and the Golden Gate Bridge. If you're on a bicycle or walking, great place for a quick stop. You can eat right there, or head over to the water, about 200 yards away, with benches and plenty of places to take your doughnuts with you. Great place for people-watching as walkers and runners all pass right by. Dynamo specializes in weird flavors, though, which may or may not be what you want. A little pricey, too. And the hours are limited, so check on that ahead of time. But it's a cool little place and a neat way to get off your feet for a bit.</Text>

<review>I wanted a particular set of wheels and tires. I searched everywhere, in other shops and online; however, none could beat the price listed at NFS. Nabeel and Sam were willing to negotiate and work within my budget.

Installation was free of charge, even wheel balancing. I noticed that I was having alignment issues due to a larger set of tires and they even fixed that free of charge. Within a week, I punctured my tire. I sent it straight to NFS and they patched it up... again... for free!

When I first came to the shop, I was hesitant because I had air suspension in my car. However, most, if not all, employees seem to run air. They gave me invaluable information about it. John even helped me roll my fenders and adjusted my ride height to perfection.

This is now my go to place. This past Winter, my tires needed a bit more air. Chris and Sulman had no issues inflating them back up and inspected them.<//review>< rate>

<text>Small shop, Josh the owner is personable and knowledgeable of trading card games. Their inventory is small compared to other shops around town but they are also one of the newer shops and one of the only remaining shops in the area. <UserId.>105687791587929823166<//UserId.>< Name>
Pmintz<//Name>
<date>1453086621218< /date><rating>5<//rating>< text>
This shop always has an event going on which is great for all card players. I recently went to their MTG prerelease tournament and everyone in the tourney ended up leaving with an extra booster pack! Their prices are pretty standard but they sell boosters for only $3. And $99 for a booster box is insanely good. Plus they offer more money on sales for store credit AND offer a rewards program!

No reason to not check this place out if you are looking for individual Magic, Pokemon, or Yu-Gi-Oh! cards. The owner Josh is really knowledgable about the cards and the rules for each game. Lastly, they have their entire inventory and buy list on their website which makes it easy to find the cards I need and know if he is buying the cards I have. Really well organized.</text>

<text>Star Wars Launch Bay is an interactive walkthrough attraction at Disneyland Park at the Disneyland Resort, Disney's Hollywood Studios at Walt Disney World Resort, and Shanghai Disneyland Park. The attraction for Disneyland Resort and Disney's Hollywood Studios was announced at D23 Expo 2015 on August 15, 2015 at the Disney Parks Presentation along with Star Wars: Galaxy's Edge, the Season of the Force events at each park, and an updated scene for Star Tours‚ÄìThe Adventures Continue. The attraction opened at each park at the start of their respective Season of the Force events, which was November 16, 2015 for Disneyland and December 4, 2015 at Disney's Hollywood Studios. The Shanghai Version opened on June 16, 2016 and closed June 2019.< /text><Pics>None< /Pics>< Resp>

<Rate>5</Rate><Review>If you are a Star Wars fan then this spot is a must visit on your Disneyland trip. There's a ton of memorabilia to see, from scaled down models of different vehicles,  to life size costumes of some of your favorite characters.
They have meet and greets with Chewbaca, Darth Vader,  and Kylo Ren. On our visit there was a small wait time depending on who you wanted to see. Chewie had the longest wait, cuz who wouldn't want to see that giant furball.
There was a small interactive gaming area where you could play some Star Wars themed games like lego Star Wars or the Star Wars Angry Birds.
It was cool seeing the full sized costumes. For an easy $3000 you could take home a nice Darth Vader outfit complete with helmet and all. I personally liked the storm troopers.
So if you get a chance,  swing by while you are in Tomorrowland.</Review>< pics>

<Rate>4<//Rate>< review>
I wanted to give this place a 5 because of how dang happy it made me, but let me break it down for ya. I absolutely loved coming here. Not a shadow of a doubt in that. Seeing all these different set pieces from the films was great! There are divided areas for things. When I went on January 14th 2018, they had a musuem, a lego section, a shop, displays, a short film, and an area to meet scheduled characters. It was all so awesome! Now, you might be thinking, well if it was so awesome why did you give it a 4? I'd say because of the size! Starwars is such a huge deal to everyone, however the size of this museum is a TAD small.

TL;DR „ÄãDespite all of this, I loved it. Perhaps one of my favorite places in Disney! If you like Starwars, I would recommend this. If you LOVE Starwars... well... WHY AREN'T YOU ALREADY THERE?!

(p.s I just found out about this "Starwars: Galaxy's Edge" theme park. I am so. so. excited.)
